```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Recruiting Transfer Students

Passed by the 2nd Student Recruitment Committee of the 2002 School Year, on December 26, 2001   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-(91)-Kao-1-Tzu No.91049202, on April 10, 2002   
Passed by the 6th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2005 School Year, on June 13, 2005   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-1-Tzu No.0940117449, on August 31, 2005   
Passed by the 4th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2012 School Year, on December 21, 2011   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-1-Tzu No.1010017098, on February 02, 2012   
Passed by the 4th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2017 School Year, on February 22, 2017   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Jao-Kao-4-Tzu No.106003006, on March 13, 2017   
Passed by the 4th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2023 School Year, November 30, 2022   
Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in Letter Tai-Kao-4-Tzu No1110127967, January 5, 2023

Article 1“Yuan Ze University Regulations for Recruiting Transfer Students” (hereafter ‘these regulations’) are provided pursuant to Article 24 of University Act, Article 19 of its Enforcement Rules as well as Regulations for Criteria of Reviewing Recruiting Procedure of Universities.

Article 2 While processing matters relating to the recruitment of transfer students, the University shall establish Transferring-student Recruitment Committee (hereafter ‘the Recruitment Committee) according to “Yuan Ze University Organizational Rules of Student Recruitment Committee”; all matters relating to the recruitment of transfer students shall be processed based on the principles of equity, justice and openness.

Article 3 If there is a vacancy for a bachelor’s program of department / college / (hereafter ‘the department’), the department may hold a transfer examination in the summer or winter vacation for recruiting transfer students to fill up the vacancy; but not for the freshmen year and senior year of study. Vacancy mentioned in the previous paragraph shall be limited to the vacancies at the department caused by insufficient registration and school withdrawal, excluding those caused by a deferral of admission, school suspension, or additional quota.

The quota for each department to fill in the vacancy shall be limited to the vacancy caused by insufficient registration and school withdrawal, excluding those caused by a deferral of admission, school suspension, or additional quota. The number of full-time teaching faculty shall be in accordance with the provisions of the Standards for Student Admission Quotas and Resources at Institutions of Higher Education.

The exact number of candidates recruited by the department shall be subject to the announcement made by each department on the exam date. The announced number of accepted candidates shall not be lower than the quota stated in student recruitment regulations.

The number of mainland Chinese transfer candidates offered admission by the department in a given academic year depends on the number of vacancies caused by insufficient registration and school withdrawal under the quota of mainland Chinese students allocated by Ministry of Education in the same academic year, and the said vacancies must not include those for general students of R.O.C. nationality or for mainland Chinese students under other levels of education. The departments that are allowed to accept mainland Chinese transfer students shall comply with the laws and regulations of Ministry of Education.

No department is allowed to divide the admission quota (or vacancies) and conduct more than one recruitment.

Article 4 The applicant qualifications for transfer student recruitment shall be administered in accordance with Article 4 of Standards for Recognition of Equivalent Educational Levels for University Admission.

The recognition of foreign academic credentials shall be complied with if a candidate’s application for taking a transfer exam. A person who received secondary school education in a foreign country shall satisfy the provisions of the Regulations Regarding the Assessment and Recognition of Foreign Academic Credentials for Institutions of Higher Education, or the Regulations Regarding the Assessment and Recognition of Academic Credentials for the Hong Kong and Macao Areas, or the Regulations Regarding the Assessment and Recognition of Academic Credentials from the Mainland Area, or Article 9 of Standards for Recognition of Equivalent Educational Levels for University Admission, as well as the regulations in student recruitment regulations.

To determine whether the departments originally majored in or credits taken by the examinees applying for the University’s transfer examination stated in the previous paragraphs are compliant with the nature of the department they intend to register for the examination and whether their grades and academic achievement (e.g. GPA) at their original schools have to be qualified, the university shall stipulate (determine) and specify it in student recruitment regulations. The University shall also include the comparison table containing information on departments (credits) sharing similar nature in student recruitment regulations as reference for examinees. Students who have been ordered to withdraw from the schooling due to unsatisfactory conduct records or disciplinary dismissal are not allowed to take the University’s transfer examination.

Article 5 While processing matters relating to the recruitment of transfer students, the University shall specify certain rules in student recruitment regulations and shall be approved by the Recruitment Committee. The student recruitment regulations shall be made public normally not later than 20 days before the University begins to accept applications.

The student recruitment regulations shall detail the departments offering admission, the prescribed duration of study, the number of vacancies, test registration requirements, exam subjects, exam dates, registration procedures, scoring criteria, methods of acceptance for admission, the preferential increasing of the total score, review of grades, check-in procedures, rules about filling vacancies by wait-listed candidates, the procedure for handling exam-related disputes, and other related rules.

Transfer examinations can be held through written test, oral test, written review, field test, or practical work.

Exam subjects, scoring methods and the percentage of each subject shall be established by the department, approved by the Recruitment Committee, and clearly stated in student recruitment regulations.

If the examination is held through oral test, field test or practical work, the process shall be tape-recorded, videotaped or recorded in writing; written records shall be completed before the Recruitment Committee decides a roll of successful candidates. If any candidate has received an extremely high or low grade, concrete reasons shall be clearly stated in the scoring sheet.

Article 6 The admission list shall be confirmed by the Recruitment Committee and officially announced by the University. The followings are admission criteria:

1. The Recruitment Committee shall determine the minimum acceptance criteria for each department before a roll of successful candidates is announced. Candidates who have satisfied the minimum acceptance criteria and are included in the admission quota will be accepted candidates, while others are wait-listed candidates.

2. If the number of applicants meeting the minimum requirements for acceptance is less than the admission quota, the vacancy may not be filled up and there are no alternates listed on the waiting list, which shall be decided by the Recruitment Committee with detailed explanations.

3. If there are any quota vacancies after the new recruits enroll into the University, the vacancy may be filled up with alternates on the waiting list before the deadline specified in student recruitment regulations. In the case that the transfer examination is held in the summer vacation, the deadline for filling up vacancies shall be by the date the enrolling semester begins which is specified in the University’s school calendar. In the case that the transfer examination is held in the winter vacation, the deadline for filling up vacancies shall be by the date the second semester of the enrolling academic year begins which is specified in the University’s school calendar.

4. If there are more than two examinees with the same total scores for the last one quota for each department, or there are alternates on the waiting list with the same total scores, the accepting standard or the order of admission for filling the vacancies shall be subject to the method stipulated in student recruitment regulations.

Article 7 In the special case of extra quota of admission, it shall be approved by Student Recruitment Committee; all the minutes from Student Recruitment Committee along with relevant documents shall be processed as the followings:

1. In the case that extra quota of admission is permitted due to examinees with the same total scores, this case shall be reported to and verified as well by the Ministry of Education within two weeks after the date the enrolling semester begins which is specified in the University’s school calendar. The Ministry of Education may adjust the recruiting quota of the department for the next school year based on whether the department is fair or not while processing the order of admission for filling the vacancies.

2. Before processing the case that extra quota of admission is permitted due to the University’s administrative negligence, a review report for student recruitment affairs shall be submitted to and verified as well by the Ministry of Education within one month after the University confirms the facts. The Ministry of Education may adjust the recruiting quota of the department for the next school year based on the seriousness of the case.

Article 8 Students being accepted shall register to the University through regulated processes, and students who fail to do so shall be regarded as giving up the acceptance. The quota vacancy may be filled up with alternates on the waiting list before the deadline which shall be by the date the enrolling semester begins and specified in the University’s school calendar.

Accepted transferring students shall submit a certificate of suspension of study, or a certificate of study, as well as relevant documents specified in student recruitment regulations when they register to the University.

Article 9 Examinees may file an appeal to Student Recruitment Committee with statements and reasons for the appeal along with written documentary evidence if they have any complaints about recruiting affairs within fifteen days of the date of notification of the result to which it relates. Any appeal filed after the time limit expires will not be accepted. After receiving the appeal, Student Recruitment Committee shall make a reply within a month; Student Recruitment Committee may establish a team for handling examinees’ appeals impartially if necessary and may inform the appellant with administrative remedy procedure.

Resolving procedures for disputes over recruitment affairs shall be processed according to “Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing Appeals of Examinees”.

Article 10 University personnel engaged in handling examinations have the obligation to keep the examination affairs confidential. No one related to the examinee within three degrees of kinship is permitted to take part in examination affairs for the principles of interest avoidance; anyone found to do so must be withdrawn from these examination affairs. All documents relating to the grading of test results shall be retained for at least one year; all documents shall be retained till the termination of the appealing or administrative remedy procedure in the case that an appeal has been filed by an examinee.

Article 11 Other relating affairs of recruiting transfer students:

1. Students being accepted shall process exemption matters according to Yuan Ze University Regulations for Credit Exemption as well as relevant regulations established by each department / college / degree program.

2. For students receiving government grants and students doing internship or service (military service) such as government sponsorship receivers of teacher preparation programs, students of military or police schools, serviceman, or policeman, they shall follow the admission procedures according to relevant regulations established by competent authorities.

3. In the case of overseas Chinese students, students from Hong Kong and Macau, or international students who have received an Alien Residence Certificate, Permanent Residence Permit, their qualifications for being examinees of the transfer examination shall be according to relevant regulations or provisions.

4. Examinees who apply for the tests with special identities must submit related certification documents and present the documents at the time of registration in order to be arranged based on the regulations for privileged examinees with different identities. Otherwise, they shall follow the requirements for regular students without privileges. Late applications for special identities with supplemental submission will not be accepted after the examination. For students who have two types of special identities, they can only select one of them for the examination.

5. Matters not specified herein shall be governed by other relevant provisions and the University’s regulations.

Article 12 These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Students Studying Elective Courses Abroad

Passed by the 2ndAcademic Affairs Meeting of the 2002 School Year, November 13, 2002   
Amended by the 1st Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2006 School Year, September 20, 2006   
Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2010 School Year, April 20, 2011   
Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2013 School Year, January 15, 2014   
Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2020 School Year, March 10, 2021

Article 1 Yuan Ze University (hereinafter referred to as “the University”) established these regulations to enhance international academic and cultural exchanges, and assist students in studying elective courses abroad.

Article 2 Overseas universities to which students apply for studying elective courses shall be those approved by the Ministry of Education; students applying for studying elective courses shall meet any of the following criteria:

1. Being recommended by the department/institute and approved by the University to go abroad to conduct research or to take credit courses at overseas universities.

2. Being selected by a governmental organization to go abroad to conduct research or to take credit courses at overseas universities.

3. Being selected by the University to become an exchange student at overseas universities with which the University has formed a cooperative partnership.

4. Being recommended by the graduate institute and approved by the University to go abroad to conduct research relating to their thesis at overseas universities.

Article 3 Students applying for studying elective courses at overseas universities shall submit the relevant application documents to the University’s authorities in the correct order for approval before going to overseas universities; students shall fill out “Application Form for Students Studying Elective Courses Abroad” as well.

Article 4 The recognition or exemption of credits for elective courses taken abroad shall be conducted according to the following stipulations:

1. Matters related to the credits taken abroad shall be conducted in accordance with the terms set forth in “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations”. Undergraduate students may be exempted from the minimum or maximum number of credit hours per semester requirement with the approval from the chairman of their department or graduate institute.

2. At the end of the study period, students shall submit the applications for recognition or exemption of credits to the University within two months after returning to Taiwan; students shall submit the original written documents including study periods, credit hours, syllabi and grade certificates of course taken.

3. Students shall submit the applications for exemption of credits after returning to the University. Any credit hours earned at overseas universities by students who have been granted a suspension of studies prior to enrolling shall be processed in accordance with “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Credit Exemption”.

4. For students studying elective courses at overseas universities and remaining enrolled at the University, all credit hours earned and grades obtained from courses taken abroad shall be processed in accordance with the regulations governing interuniversity course selection. The total credit hours earned and grades obtained shall be recorded on the students’ overall transcripts.

5. For students studying elective courses at overseas universities, all credit hours earned from courses taken abroad shall come along with the grade certificates issued by the institute where the courses are taken; the Chinese title and the content of courses taken shall be reviewed by the chairman of their department or graduate institute and approved by Office of Academic Affairs.

6. Whether or not credit hours earned overseas are to be counted toward the students’ credit hours required for graduation shall be determined by each department or graduate institute separately.

7. For the calculation of credits, one credit will be calculated after 18 hours of teaching in a semester. For conversion of credits from foreign academic systems, please refer to the following table:

<table><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1></td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Yuan ZeUniversity</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>American system,Japanese system,Chinese system</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>EuropeanCreditTransfer andAccumulationSystem</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>The accumulatedof UK creditsand conversionsystem</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Units</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Credit</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Credit</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>ECTS</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>CATS</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>ConversionRatio</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>1</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>1</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>2</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>4</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=5>Note: The abovecreditconversionratiois ageneralrule.Thenalcrditconversiondetermination is calculated and reviewed by the relevant competent authority.</td></tr></table>

Article 5 Recorded credit hours earned and grades obtained from courses taken at overseas universities shall be processed according to the following stipulations:

1. Calculation of students’ grades shall be based on the grade certificates issued by the institute where the courses are taken. Grade conversions shall be conducted in accordance with the cross reference of grade scale and 100-mark scale set forth in “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations”. The original grade certificates shall be submitted to Registration Section and retained on file for reference.

2. When converting credit hours, for each 18 hours of completed course taken it is considered one credit hour into the University’s credits.

3. Grades not showed in 100-mark scale can be converted to 100-mark scale based on the cross reference provided by the institute where the courses are taken and then recorded on the transcript.

4. In the case that the institute where the courses are taken fails to provide the cross reference for 100-mark scale, grade conversions shall be conducted based on the following table:

<table><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Undergraduate</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>96</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>90</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>84</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>78</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>75</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>72</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>68</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>65</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>62</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>50</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1></td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A+</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B+</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C+$</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>D</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Graduate</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>96</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>90</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>86</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>84</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>80</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>76</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>74</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>70</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>66</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>50</td></tr></table>

5. In the case that the grade from the institute where the courses are taken is Low Pass (50 as Pass), the recorded grade in the University will be converted as: 60 + (the grade of the institute-50)\*40/50.

6. In the case that the grade can not be converted in accordance with the preceding statement as in 4 and 5, students shall submit documents or proof of grades that can be converted or recorded; in the case that the grade (such as Pass or Satisfactory) can not be converted in any forms, 70 will be given as the grade for undergraduate students and 80 will be given as the grade for graduate students.

Article 6 Other matters not stipulated in these regulations shall be conducted in accordance with “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations” and other relevant rules.

Article 7 These regulations are adopted by Academic Affairs Meeting, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations Governing the Conferral of An Honorary Doctoral Degree

Passed by the temporary College Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 1992, on July 20, 1993   
Amended by the 1st University Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2002, on January 8, 2003   
Amended by the 2nd University Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2002, on June 25, 2003

## Article 1 Establishment of regulations

These regulations are provided pursuant to Degree Conferral Law and its Enforcement Rules established by Ministry of Education.

Article 2 Qualifications for being a candidate for an honorary doctoral degree:

Professor meeting any one of the following conditions may be a candidate for an honorary doctoral degree:

1. has achieved outstanding academic or professional accomplishments or contributions that benefit mankind.

2. has made an important contribution to culture, academic exchange, or world peace.

## Article 3 Objects of the conferral:

The conferral shall be limited to the current conferral of doctoral degrees at the university.

Article 4 The conferral of an honorary doctoral degree shall get the consent from the recommended candidate first. Personnel concerned have the obligation to keep the list of candidates confidential during the selection procedure (including recommendation, first review and final review).

## Article 5 First review:

The president shall establish a first review team, which shall provide the list of qualified candidates to College Council Meeting for further recommendation procedure.

The first review team referred to in the preceding paragraph shall be composed of the president, Academic Dean, the dean of the relevant college, Chief Secretary. Board member delegates and relevant personnel outside the University may attend the meeting held by the team. The president shall be the convener as well as the chairman.

## Article 6 Final review:

Candidates for an honorary doctoral degree shall be recommended by College Council Meeting and then submitted to the university’s review committee for an honorary doctoral degree for the final review.

The review committee referred to in the preceding paragraph shall be chaired by the university president, and its membership shall be composed of five to seven members, including Academic Dean, the dean of the relevant college/graduate school/department, and faculty delegates appointed by the president.

Article 7 An honorary doctoral degree established by the university must approve such a degree after the final review, which upon conferral shall be reported to the Ministry of Education for recordation.

The approved list of the conferral of an honorary doctoral degree being reported to the Ministry of Education for recordation shall include the following information of conferees: name, sex, birth date, nationality, educational background, working experience, title of degree being conferred, and the qualifications as well as detailed statements mentioned in Article 2 of these regulations.

Article 8 The graduation gown, diploma format, and conferral ceremony for an honorary doctoral degree shall be established separately.

Article 9 These regulations are adopted by School Council Meeting, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Student Conduct in Recruiting Examinations

Passed by the 5th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2003 School Year, on May 19, 2004

Amended by the 3rd Student Recruitment Committee of the 2004 School Year, on April 26, 2005

Amended by the 4th Student Recruitment Committee of the 2004 School Year, on May 19, 2005

Amended by the 2nd Student Recruitment Committee of the 2005 School Year, on October 11, 2005 Amended

by the 1st Student Recruitment Committee of the 2007 School Year, on September 13, 2006

1. Examinees shall enter the exam room with admission cards at the scheduled exam time and take the seat assigned according to their examinee numbers. Examinees shall not enter the exam room before the exam starts; examinees shall not stay outside the exam room in the hallway after the preparation bell rings. Examinees shall not be admitted into the exam room for arriving more than 20 minutes (30 minutes for the first session) after the exam begins; examinees shall not be admitted to leave the room within 40 minutes of the total duration. Examinees who enter the wrong exam room shall not leave without permission; they shall raise their hands and report to the proctor for further instructions.

2. Examinees shall put admission cards at the upper/left hand side of the desk and check the consistency among the answering sheet, assigned seat and examinee number. Examinees shall raise their hands to inform the proctor of any inconsistency or missing items.

3. Examinees shall not request the proctor to answer inquiries on test questions except for that the test questions have been too poorly printed to be legible. In that case, examinees may raise their hands and ask the proctor to resolve the problem. If an examinee accidentally drops the test paper onto the ground, he/she shall first raise his/her hands to inform the proctor and then pick it up.

4. If examinees have any of the following circumstances, their qualifications for taking the exam shall be deprived, their grades of exam subjects that have been taken shall be counted as 0, and they shall not be allowed to take any other exam subjects afterwards:

(1) Examinees not entering or leaving the exam room at the regulated exam time.

(2) Examinees being impostors or holding fake examination identities.

(3) Examinees exchanging seats or answer sheets with each other.

(4) Examinees passing on or carrying related documents or reference materials; writing (copy) relevant words or signs on the desk, admission card, body, or other objects.

(5) Examinees threatening other examinees to help them cheat or intimidating proctors.

(6) Examinees staying outside the exam room after handing in the answering sheet, disturbing the order of the exam site, and not following the proctor’s instructions after being warned for twice.

5. If examinees have any of the following circumstances, their grades shall be deducted 20 points or even be counted as 0, depends on the situation:

(1) Examinees talking to each other during the test, intending to look at and copy other examinees answers, or allowing others to see their answers deliberately.

(2) Examinees breaking or damaging the seal of the answer sheet.

(3) Examinees tearing out the answer sheet, writing their names or using the seal on the answer sheet to identify themselves.

(4) Examinees smoking, drinking or eating at the exam site and not following the proctor’s instructions after being warned for twice.

(5) Examinees changing the answers after leaving their seats or giving their answer sheets to others to hand in for them.

(6) Examinees leaving the exam room with the answer sheet or test questions.

(7) Examinees not taking the make-up test at the regulated exam time after being informed.

6. If examinees have any of the following circumstances, their grades shall be deducted 5 points or even be counted as 0, depends on the situation:

(1) Examinees entering the exam room without their admission cards may be permitted to take the exam after a proctor has verified the identity. However, those who don’t get their admission cards delivered before the ending bell rings or those who don’t apply to the university’s test administration center for the reissue of admission card before the test session begins, their grades shall be deducted 5 points or even be counted as 0.

(2) Examinees taking the wrong seat and answering on the incorrect answer sheet due to that they don’t take the assigned seat or check the consistency among the answering sheet, assigned seat number, examinee number, test subject, and test paper before answering the test questions.

(3) Examinees damaging, folding, tucking the answer sheet or writing any words or symbols that are irrelevant to test answers on the answer sheet.

(4) Examinees not using blue or black fountain pens, or pencils to draw graphs or write words except for the special regulations of certain test questions.

(5) Examinees not stop writing immediately when the ending bell rings.

(6) Examinees not complying with the regulated procedures in answering questions.

(7) Examinees bringing things that may disturb the order of the exam site or affect the fairness of the test such as calculator, book, handout, pager, cell phone or any other electronic telecommunication devices, except for necessary stationary or regulated calculator for specific usage.

(8) Examinees entering the exam room without bringing the proof of their identities with photos such as ID cards, driving licenses, or health insurance cards.

7. Examinees not answering the test questions on the regulated answer sheets shall not be graded.

8. Examinees not being graded due to the lost or damage of their answer sheets which have been handed in after the test shall be granted to take the make-up test at the regulated exam time after being informed.

9. Proctors or exam administration personnel have the right to check any suspicious personal belongings and to take actions toward any misconduct that may disturb the order of the exam site or affect the fairness of the test. Examinees may be asked to provide their signatures or to be photographed as evidence, and examinees’ qualifications shall be canceled if they refuse to do so. In this case, examinees shall not raise objections or ask for extra points or require an extension of exam time.

10. Any examinees who engage in any form of misbehavior not specifically proscribed by aforementioned regulations may be cited by a proctor and brought to the attention of Student Recruitment Committee for adopting appropriate measures depends on the situation. Examinees engaging in any form of misbehavior and attempting to eliminate evidence may be proved by a proctor to be true and brought to the attention of the school for adopting measures in accordance with these regulations depends on the situation.

11. If there is a postponement of the exam due to the occurring of typhoon or earthquake or other force majeure, the postponement will be announced by the school and be broadcast through TV or radio stations as well. However, examinees will not be informed of the postponement individually.

12. These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Establishing Academic Credit Programs

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2004, on April 28, 2004   
Amended by the 1st Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2006, on September 20, 2006   
Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2007, on November 7, 2007   
Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2009, on November 4, 2009   
Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs meeting, Academic Year 2012, on March 7, 2012   
Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs meeting, Academic Year 2017, on November 15, 2017   
Amended by the 7nd Academic Affairs meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 31, 2023   
Amended by the 7nd Academic Affairs meeting, Academic Year 2024, on March 20,2024   
Amended by the 3rd Academic Affairs meeting, Academic Year 2024, on December 25,2024

1. The regulations established aim to provide a standard guideline when setting up academic credit programs in academic units. The course programs stated in the regulations are referred to the design and combination of cross department/school/college curriculum in all professional learning fields and are offered as an interdisciplinary field that combines courses from two or more degree programs or academic credit programs. Academic credit programs should invite an Assistant Professor, Associate Professor, or Professor, as the director of the academic credit programs, to be in charge of establishing academic credit programs, handling promotion activities and issuing certificate; besides, the academic unit which the director of academic credit programs belongs to should take charge of the general administrative affairs of academic credit programs. Academic credit programs can set up an Academic Credit Program Committee if needed.

2. The Academic Credit Programs of the school are divided into Normal Program and Micro-Program. For the Normal Program, the student shall select at least 12 credits, and for the Micro-Program shall select at least 8 credits. To establish the academic credit programs, the relevant regulations on matters—objectives, program title, curriculum plan, required subjects and credits thereof, director of academic credit programs, eligibility, student numbers, approval process, application deadline and certificates of academic credit programs and standard thereof must be established by academic units in charge and must be adopted by the Curriculum Committee Meeting and the Academic Affairs Meeting for ratification and implementation before announcement, as shall amendments when they are made.

Yuan Ze University Industry-Academia Programs are divided into "Enterprise Programs" and "Industry Programs". The names, content, and implementation methods of these programs are conducted in accordance with the regulations stipulated in the "Yuan Ze University Regulations for the Establishment of Industry-Academia Programs ".

3. The minimum credits required for graduation will not be increased due to studying academic credit programs. Moreover, students cannot apply for extending study period due to studying academic credit programs except as provided in other regulations.

4. Students who intend to study the academic credit programs should meet all required conditions, register online for studying academic credit programs in the application period and receive the approval of the application from academic units in charge of academic credit programs. Then, students can select courses of academic credit programs online.

5. In order to obtain the certificates of the academic credit programs, students who complete all required subjects and receive all credits for those courses can file an application with their official transcripts enclosed to colleges at which the academic credit programs are offered and receive the approval of the application afterwards. The certificates won’t be available for students who do not register for studying the course programs in advance.

6. All applications for academic credit programs must be filed online. The format for the certificate of academic credit programs is designed and set up by Academic Affairs Office except as provided in other regulations.

7. If the academic credit programs cannot be offered due to the change of educational objectives, the transition of industrial development or other factors, the units in charge of these programs can alter the programs’ contents or cancel the programs based on the original approved procedures. If the number of students enrolled in the academic credit programs is less than 10 in a consecutive of 3 academic years, the Office of Academic Affairs can call a meeting to reevaluate the establishment of these programs. The programs can be called off after the re-evaluation being approved by the Curriculum Committee Meeting and passed at the Academic Affairs Meeting afterwards.

8. In order to cooperate with the Ministry of Education to promote the "Taiwan Artificial Intelligence College Alliance" (TAICA) plan, the establishment of the alliance's AI course, number of credits, application procedures and certificate issuance methods shall be based on relevant regulations. Regulations

9. These regulations will be adopted by the Academic Affairs Meeting before implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Directions of Teaching Hours Deduction for Supervisors

Passed by the 2nd Administrative Council of Academic Year 2005 on 2005-09-12   
Amended by the 3rd Administrative Council of Academic Year 2008 on 2008-10-06   
Amended by the 8th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2012 on 2012-12-03   
Amended by the 20th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2017 on 2018-06-06   
Amended by the 10th Administrative Council of Academic Year 2023 on 2023-12-13

1. The Directions on Teaching Hours Deduction for Supervisors are formulated in accordance with Article 7 of “Yuan Ze University Regulations for Faculty’s Teaching Hours and Deduction”.

2. The teaching hours deduction for academic and administrative executives will be implemented based on the provisions of these directions.

3. Supervisors who hold two positions concurrently shall have their teaching hours deducted based on the higher position. In order to avoid affecting the arrangement for instructors and protect students' right to education, the supervisors who are appointed after the beginning of classes will have their teaching hours deducted and effective from the next semester.

Overtime hours in the fall semester can be applied to be retained until the spring semester of the same academic year.

## 4. List of Teaching Hours Deductions for All Supervisors:

<table><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Title</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Teaching Hours Deduction</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>President, Vice President</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>No course to lecture</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Dean of Academic Affairs,Dean of Student Aff airs,Dean of General Affairs,Dean of Research and Development,Dean of Library and Information Services,Dean of Global Afairs Office,Deans of Colleges,Secretary General,Director of Lifelong Education,Director of General Studies</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>1 course /per semester3 hours overtime pay /per academic year</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Chairpersons of Departments (or the units at thesame level),Director, Deans of Academies, Vice Dean,Section Chief(orthesupervisoof unt athesame level),Director of_EnvironmentalProtection andOccupational Safety and Health Center</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>4 teaching hours deduction /per semester2 hours overtime pay /per semester</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Director of the Center in Item 2 of Article 6</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>2 teaching hours deduction /per semester2 hours overtime pay /per semester</td></tr></table>

5. The supervisors who are entitled to lecture one course per semester have to lecture at least one complete course with 2 or more credits per semester.

6. Director in Article 4 includes Director of: Personnel Office, General Accounting Office, Physical Education Office, and Military Education Office.

Director of the Center in Article 4 includes the supervisors of: Art Center, Management Competency Development and Research Center, and each center included in the Research Unit.

7. The supervisor of the preparatory unit should submit documents to the president for approval of teaching hours deduction until the unit is formally established.

8. The directions shall be promulgated and implemented after being passed by the Executive Council Meeting. Amendments of the directions shall follow the same procedures.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Admission of Undergraduate Students through High School Recommendation

Passed by the 3rd Student Recruitment Committee Meeting, Academic Year 2007, on December 27, 2006 Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in the Letter Tai-Kao-1-Tzu No.0960017327, on January 31, 2007

## Article 1 Establishment:

These regulations are provided pursuant to Article 24 of University Act as well as Article 19 of its Enforcement Rules.

## Article 2 Student Recruitment Committee:

Student Recruitment Committee shall be established according to “Organizational Rules of Student Recruitment Committee”; matters relating to the recruitment of students shall be specified in student recruitment regulations and shall be processed based on the principles of equity, justice and openness.

## Article 3 Quota of admission:

Quota of admission for each department/college/institute shall be based on the university’s yearly quota for each department/college/institute that has been gone through the verification process and been approved by the Ministry of Education.

## Article 4 Qualifications of admission:

Students with the following two qualifications can be recommended by their senior high schools to apply for admission through recommendation. Relevant regulations regarding the recommendation shall be established by each high school concerned.

1. Being graduates of the present year with three-year study in the same senior high school and the schools shall be the ones listed in the student recruitment regulations published by College Admissions Committee.

2. Being examinees of Scholastic Achievement English Test (SAET) held by College Entrance Examination Center (CEEC) with grades meeting the basic requirements made by departments of the university and specified in student recruitment regulations.

## Article 5 Examining methods:

1. The university’s departments shall be divided into at most three academic groups to recruit students.

2. Senior high schools shall divide students into different academic groups and recommend one qualified student of each academic group according to the admission requirement of each department. Moreover, one student shall be recommended to one academic group only. The university shall determine the limited number of departments of each academic group to be filled in by one student, and only one student of each senior high school can be admitted into the university.

## Article 6 Admission criteria:

1. Criteria may be based on the grade of a particular subject of Scholastic Achievement English Test such as Chinese, English, Math, Social Science, Physics or Chemistry; criteria may also be based on the rank of overall grade of Scholastic Achievement English Test announced by College Entrance Examination Center such as Top Percentile Rank, Second-highest Percentile Rank, Average Percentile Rank, Second-lowest Percentile Rank, and Bottom Percentile Rank.

2. The order of admission shall be based on students’ school ranking percentage of total grades average of each semester in the first and the second years of senior high school. The priority of admission shall be given to the students of the smallest percentage.

3. For students of the same percentage stated in the previous paragraph, the order shall be compared according to the requirements established by each department. In case of the same result after the aforementioned comparison, the students shall all be enrolled.

Article 7 In the special case of extra quota of admission, it shall be approved by Student Recruitment Committee; all the minutes from Student Recruitment Committee along with relevant documents shall be reported to and verified as well by the Ministry of Education before the enrollment of new recruits. In the case that extra quota of admission is permitted due to administrative negligence, a review report for student recruitment affairs shall be submitted.

Article 8 Students being admitted into the university must not apply for the following school entrance methods such as university admission through selection, university admission through entrance examination, or joint admissions for colleges by registration and placement. Those who fail to do so will be disqualified for being admitted into the university except for those who have requested the university to relinquish their qualifications. If there is still quota vacancy for this admission method, the vacancy can be filled up through college entrance examination.

Article 10 University personnel engaged in handling examinations have the obligation to keep the examination affairs confidential. No one related to the examinee within three degrees of kinship is permitted to take part in examination affairs for the principles of interest avoidance; anyone found to do so must be withdrawn from these examination affairs. All documents relating to the grading of test results shall be retained for at least one year; all documents shall be retained till the termination of the appealing or administrative remedy procedure in the case that an appeal has been filed by an examinee.

Article 11 These regulations will be adopted by the university’s Student Recruitment Committee before being reported to the Ministry of Education for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

```markdown
# Yuan Ze University Regulations for Students Taking Courses from Overseas Universities in Taiwan

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2006 School Year, July 4, 2007   
Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2012 School Year, March 7, 2012   
Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2013 School Year, January 15, 2014   
Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting of the 2020 School Year, March 10, 2021

Article 1 Yuan Ze University (hereinafter referred to as “the University”) established these regulations to enhance international academic and cultural exchanges, and assist students in taking courses from overseas universities in Taiwan.

Article 2 Overseas universities to which students apply for taking courses from shall be those approved by the Ministry of Education; students applying for taking courses from overseas universities in Taiwan shall be those who are recommended by the department/institute and approved by the University.

Article 3 Students applying for taking courses from overseas universities in Taiwan shall submit the relevant application documents to the University’s authorities in the correct order for approval before doing so; students shall fill out “Application Form for Students Taking Courses from Overseas Universities in Taiwan” as well.

Article 4 The recognition of credits taken from overseas universities in Taiwan shall be conducted according to the following stipulations:

1. At the end of the study period, students shall submit the applications for recognition of credits to the University; students shall submit the original written documents including study periods, credit hours, syllabi and grade certificates of course taken.

2. Credit hours earned and grades obtained from overseas universities in Taiwan shall be processed in accordance with the regulations governing interuniversity course selection. The total credit hours earned and grades obtained shall be recorded on the students’ overall transcripts.

3. Credit hours earned from overseas universities in Taiwan shall come along with the grade certificates issued by the institute where the courses are taken; the Chinese title and the content of courses taken shall be reviewed by the chairman of their department or graduate institute and approved by Office of Academic Affairs.

4. Credit hours earned from overseas universities in Taiwan shall be calculated into the credits students taking that semester and shall be processed in accordance with “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations”.

5. Credits earned by students for courses taken at overseas universities or colleges must be supported by official transcripts issued by the host institution. The Chinese course titles and content must be reviewed by the department chair or program director and approved by the Office of Academic Affairs.

6. Whether the course credits are counted toward the total graduation credits will be determined

by the respective department or program.

7. At this university, one credit is awarded for every 18 hours of instruction per semester. Credit conversion for foreign education systems can be referred to in the table below.

<table><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1></td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>YZU</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>US System,Japan System,China System</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>EuropeanCredit TransferandAccumulationSystem</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>UK CreditAccumulation and TransferSystem</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>unit</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Credit</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Credit</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>ECTS</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>CATS</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>conversion ratio</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>1</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>1</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>2</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>4</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=5>Note: heabovecrdtonvonorealuili.Fialcrdtcorecognition and approval will be determined by the relevant administrative units.</td></tr></table>

Article 5 Recorded credit hours earned and grades obtained from overseas universities in Taiwan shall be processed according to the following stipulations:

1. Calculation of students’ grades shall be based on the grade certificates issued by the institute where the courses are taken. Grade conversions shall be conducted in accordance with the cross reference of grade scale and 100-mark scale set forth in “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations”. The original grade certificates shall be submitted to Registration Section and retained on file for reference.

2. Due to the differences between domestic and foreign academic systems, the recognition of credit hours shall be determined by each department or graduate institute separately and then approved by Office of Academic Affairs.

3. Grades not showed in 100-mark scale can be converted to 100-mark scale based on the cross reference provided by the institute where the courses are taken and then recorded on the transcript.

4. In the case that the institute where the courses are taken fails to provide the cross reference for 100-mark scale, grade conversions shall be conducted based on the following table:

<table><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Undergraduate</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>96</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>90</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>84</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>78</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>75</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>72</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>68</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>65</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>62</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>50</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1></td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A+$</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B+</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C+</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>D</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Graduate</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>96</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>90</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>86</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>84</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>80</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>76</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>74</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>70</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>66</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>50</td></tr></table>

5. In the case that the grade from the institute where the courses are taken is Low Pass (50 as Pass), the recorded grade in the University will be converted as: 60 + (the grade of the institute-50)\*40/50.

6. In the case that the grade can not be converted in accordance with the preceding statement as in 4 and 5, students shall submit documents or proof of grades that can be converted or recorded; in the case that the grade (such as Pass or Satisfactory) can not be converted in any forms, 70 will be given as the grade for undergraduate students and 80 will be given as the grade for graduate students.

Article 6 Other matters not stipulated in these regulations shall be conducted in accordance with “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations” and other relevant rules.

Article 7 These regulations are adopted by Academic Affairs Meeting, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.

7. Calculation of students’ grades shall be based on the grade certificates issued by the institute where the courses are taken. Grade conversions shall be conducted in accordance with the cross reference of grade scale and 100-mark scale set forth in “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations”. The original grade certificates shall be submitted to Registration Section and retained on file for reference.

8. Due to the differences between domestic and foreign academic systems, the recognition of credit hours shall be determined by each department or graduate institute separately and then approved by Office of Academic Affairs.

9. Grades not showed in 100-mark scale can be converted to 100-mark scale based on the cross reference provided by the institute where the courses are taken and then recorded on the transcript.

10. In the case that the institute where the courses are taken fails to provide the cross reference for 100-mark scale, grade conversions shall be conducted based on the following table:

<table><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Undergraduate</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>96</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>90</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>84</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>78</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>75</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>72</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>68</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>65</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>62</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>50</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1></td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A+</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>A-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B+</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>B-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C+</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>C-</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>D</td></tr><tr><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>Graduate</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>96</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>90</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>86</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>84</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>80</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>76</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>74</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>70</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>66</td><td rowspan=1 colspan=1>50</td></tr></table>

11. In the case that the grade from the institute where the courses are taken is Low Pass (50 as Pass), the recorded grade in the University will be converted as: 60 + (the grade of the institute-50)\*40/50.

12. In the case that the grade can not be converted in accordance with the preceding statement as in 4 and 5, students shall submit documents or proof of grades that can be converted or recorded; in the case that the grade (such as Pass or Satisfactory) can not be converted in any forms, 70 will be given as the grade for undergraduate students and 80 will be given as the grade for graduate students.

Article 6 Other matters not stipulated in these regulations shall be conducted in accordance with “Yuan Ze University Study Regulations” and other relevant rules.

Article 7 These regulations are adopted by Academic Affairs Meeting, as shall amendments when they are made.

If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

#### OCR 39: http://www.yzu.edu.tw/admin/so/files/regulations/c%20en/1-60.pdf

```markdown
## Yuan Ze University Regulations for Admission into College, Department, Degree Program through Senior Vocational School Recommendation and Selection

Passed by the 3rd Student Recruitment Committee Meeting, Academic Year 2010, on December 24, 2009 Approved for future reference by Ministry of Education in the Letter Tai-Gi-2-Tzu No.0990006388, on January 21, 2010

1. These regulations are established pursuant to “Regulations for Admission into Two-year or Four-year Program of Junior College through Recommendation And Selection” constituted by the Ministry of Education. The purpose of these regulations are to pursue aptitude- and expertise- based development of students, to ensure the independence for recruiting students of each college/department/degree program, and to process matters relating to the recruitment of students based on the principles of equity, justice and openness.

2. “Admission through recommendation and selection” mentioned in these regulations refers to the recommendations made by senior vocational schools of eligible graduates of the present year who meet the qualifications required by the university’s colleges, departments or degree programs. Those graduates will be admitted into the university via the selection process done by Technological and Vocational College Joint Selection Committee based on their grades of Joint Achievement Test.

3. Colleges, departments or degree programs shall list basic requirements and relevant notifications such as qualifications, screening subjects, screening criteria, verification of certificates or licenses, admission methods, admission quotas, send to Office of Academic Affairs for coordination, submit to Student Recruitment Committee for approval before being put into student recruitment regulations. Matters relating to the designated subjects of screening shall be processed based on relevant regulations.

4. Matters relating to the screening affairs shall be processed in the following procedures:

(1) Graduates of the present year will be screened through basic requirements made by colleges/departments/degree programs via the selection process done by Technological and Vocational College Joint Selection Committee based on their grades of Joint Achievement Test. After the committee sends the university grades and relevant documents of students who meet the basic requirements, Office of Academic Affairs shall notify those students as well as their vocational schools to take part in the designated subjects of screening test held by the university.

(2) Verification of certificates or licenses: After registering for the designated subjects of screening test, eligible graduates recommended by their schools shall submit their award certificates/proofs of skills competition and their Technician Certificates to the university. Colleges/departments/degree programs as well as Technological and Vocational College Joint Selection Committee shall verify these certificates to see if the graduates meet the requirement for getting extra points.

(3) Designated subjects of screening test: The following affairs shall be established by colleges/departments/degree programs and submitted to Student Recruitment Committee for approval.

a. Designated subjects may include written test, interview, field test, practical work, or review of the qualification of graduates being recommended.

b. Holding of the screening test: One to four designated subjects shall be adopted for the screening test which shall be done within two-day period. The recommendation-related documents (including reference documents) submitted by eligible graduates shall be included in the scoring of designated items or provided as reference for interview by colleges/departments/degree programs.

c. Place and time of the screening test shall be decided by colleges/departments/degree programs and submitted to Student Recruitment Committee for arrangement.

d. Grading criteria shall be established and put into student recruitment regulations as reference.

(4) Announcement of admission: Student Recruitment Committee shall establish the minimum admission requirements and the admission shall be determined by the total grades of examinees which include grades of Joint Achievement Test, grades of designated subjects of screening test, high school grades, extra points earned through attending skills competition with awards or certificates. The admission list and a copy of grades list of screening test shall be announced by the university and shall be submitted to Technological and Vocational College Joint Selection Committee. The following documents shall be sent by the university to senior vocational schools and then shall be passed to the schools’ students: grades of screening test received by examinees, notification of admission, regulations for inquiring the grade of screening test.

5. According to the regulations of the Ministry of Education, universities receiving “Award for Teaching Excellence Project” can recruit students of senior vocational schools with additional quota of one to five students.

6. Examination affairs of screening tests shall be processed in the following methods:

(1) Test questions of written tests of the designated subjects shall be generated by relevant faculties appointed by the dean or chairman of colleges/departments/degree programs. University personnel engaged in handling examinations are responsible for making the sealed list of examinees, admission cards, test questions and test papers.

(2) Interview, field test, practical work or other test methods shall be processed by colleges/departments/degree programs based on relevant regulations.

(3) Colleges/departments/degree programs shall submit the examinees’ grades reports of designated subjects of screening test as well as other relevant documents to Office of Academic Affairs for the counting of total grades of examinees according to their performance of screening tests and the university’s grading criteria. Office of Academic Affairs shall make the grades list of examinees of colleges/departments/degree programs in sequence from high to low and the list shall be submitted to Student Recruitment Committee which shall hold a meeting to make decisions about the minimum requirements for acceptance as well as the quota of admission.

The priority of acceptance shall be determined by the total grades of examinees in sequence from high to low; those who don’t meet the minimum requirements for acceptance shall not be accepted even there is quota vacancy. For the same total score, the order of admission shall be subject to the method stipulated in student recruitment regulations. 7. Students being admitted into the university through recommendation and selection must not apply for taking part in joint admissions for colleges by registration and placement except for those who have made a written request for the university to relinquish their qualifications. 8. Students being admitted into the university through recommendation and selection may apply for change of major beginning from the second year of study; students may also take a school transfer examination based on their needs of study. 9. These regulations will be adopted by Student Recruitment Committee for ratification and implementation, as shall amendments when they are made. If any controversies or disputes occurred regarding clauses of the contract, it shall always refer to its Chinese version.
```

#### OCR 40: http://www.yzu.edu.tw/admin/so/files/regulations/c%20en/1-61.pdf

- 本機檔案: admin/so/files/regulations/c en/1-61.pdf

- OCR 字數: 15950
